				}

			subtract_from_variable = { treasury = 1.5 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = 1_5_billion_expense_tt
			every_other_country = {
				hidden_effect = {
					set_temp_variable = { influence_gain = 2 }
					for_loop_effect = {
						end = influence_array^num
						value = v
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { influence_array^v = CHI }
							}
							add_to_variable = { influence_array_val^v = influence_gain }
							set_country_flag = found
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = found } }
							add_to_array = { influence_array = CHI.id }
							add_to_array = { influence_array_val = influence_gain }
					}
					clr_country_flag = found
					recalculate_influence = yes
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = CHI_small_influence_tt
			}
			log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: focus CHI_Set_up_Confucius_Institutes executed"

		prerequisite = { focus = CHI_Purge_the_Communist_Party }
		prerequisite = { focus = CHI_Proper_State_Nationalization }
		mutually_exclusive = { focus = CHI_Revolution_in_One_Country }
		
		available = {
			has_government = communism
			communism > 0.8
			NOT = {
				has_idea = factional_politics_elitist
				has_idea = three_represents
				has_idea = zeng_qinghong_thought
				has_idea = industrial_conglomerates
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = the_military has_idea = communist_cadres }
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = CHI_minimum_opinion_enthusiastic_tt
					has_country_flag = enthusiastic_the_military
					has_country_flag = enthusiastic_communist_cadres
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = the_military NOT = { has_idea = communist_cadres } }
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = CHI_minimum_opinion_enthusiastic_PLA_tt
					has_country_flag = enthusiastic_the_military
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_idea = the_military } has_idea = communist_cadres }
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = CHI_minimum_opinion_enthusiastic_CC_tt
					has_country_flag = enthusiastic_communist_cadres
				}
			}
		}
		
		completion_reward = {
			add_war_support = 0.05
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { party_pop_array^4 > 0.05 }
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = CHI_small_influence_10_tt
				hidden_effect = {
					set_temp_variable = { influence_gain = 10 }
					for_loop_effect = {
						end = influence_array^num
						value = v
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { influence_array^v = CHI }
							}
							add_to_variable = { influence_array_val^v = influence_gain }
							set_country_flag = found
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = found } }
							add_to_array = { influence_array = CHI.id }
							add_to_array = { influence_array_val = influence_gain }
					}
					clr_country_flag = found
					recalculate_influence = yes
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = CHI_fifth_international_5_tt
				hidden_effect = {
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = communism
						popularity = 0.05
					}
					add_to_variable = {
						var = party_pop_array^4
						value = 0.05
					}
					recalculate_party = yes
				}
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = Socialist_Market_Economy_planned_2
				add_idea = Planned_Economy
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				every_country = {
					news_event = { id = china.32 }
				}
			}
			increase_centralization = yes
			log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: focus CHI_Form_the_Fifth_International executed"
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 100
		}
	}

				set_temp_variable = { influence_gain = 10 }
				for_loop_effect = {
					end = influence_array^num
					value = v
					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { influence_array^v = KOR }
						}
						add_to_variable = { influence_array_val^v = influence_gain }
						set_country_flag = found
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = found } }
						add_to_array = { influence_array = KOR.id }
						add_to_array = { influence_array_val = influence_gain }
				}
				clr_country_flag = found
				recalculate_influence = yes
			}
			KOR = {
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = CHI
					modifier = improve_trade
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = CHI_small_influence_10_tt
				hidden_effect = {
					set_temp_variable = { influence_gain = 10 }
					for_loop_effect = {
						end = influence_array^num
						value = v
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { influence_array^v = CHI }
							}
							add_to_variable = { influence_array_val^v = influence_gain }
							set_country_flag = found
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = found } }
							add_to_array = { influence_array = CHI.id }
							add_to_array = { influence_array_val = influence_gain }
					}
					clr_country_flag = found
					recalculate_influence = yes
				}
			}
			log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: focus CHI_China_Republic_of_Korea_Free_Trade_Agreement executed"
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 100
		}
	}

							array = influence_array
							value = v
							index = i
							if = {
								limit = { var:v = { tag = CHI } }
								set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = i }
								always = yes
							}
							else = { always = no }
						}
					check_variable = { temp_idx > -1 }
					check_variable = { influence_array_calc^temp_idx > 0.4 }
				}
			}
		}
